These classes should be explicitly instantiated for any IR unit,\n/// and files doing the explicit instantiation should include this header.\n///\n//===----------------------------------------------------------------------===//\n\n#ifndef LLVM_IR_PASSMANAGERIMPL_H\n#define LLVM_IR_PASSMANAGERIMPL_H\n\n#include \"llvm/IR/Function.h\"\n#include \"llvm/IR/PassInstrumentation.h\"\n#include \"llvm/IR/PassManager.h\"\n#include \"llvm/Support/CommandLine.h\"\n#include \"llvm/Support/Compiler.h\"\n#include \"llvm/Support/PrettyStackTrace.h\"\n\nnamespace llvm {\n\ntemplate <typename IRUnitT, typename AnalysisManagerT, typename... ExtraArgTs>\nPreservedAnalyses PassManager<IRUnitT, AnalysisManagerT, ExtraArgTs...>::run(\n    IRUnitT &IR, AnalysisManagerT &AM, ExtraArgTs... ExtraArgs) {\n  class StackTraceEntry : public PrettyStackTraceEntry {\n    const PassInstrumentation &PI;\n    IRUnitT &IR;\n    PassConceptT *Pass = nullptr;\n\n  public:\n    explicit StackTraceEntry(const PassInstrumentation &PI, IRUnitT &IR)\n        : PI(PI), IR(IR) {}\n\n    void setPass(PassConceptT *P) { Pass = P; }\n\n    void print(raw_ostream &OS) const override {\n      OS << \"Running pass \\\"\";\n      if (Pass)\n        Pass->printPipeline(OS, [this](StringRef ClassName) {\n          auto PassName = PI.getPassNameForClassName(ClassName);\n          return PassName.empty() ? ClassName : PassName;\n        });\n      else\n        OS << \"unknown\";\n      OS << \"\\\" on \";\n      printIRUnitNameForStackTrace(OS, IR);\n      OS << \"\\n\";\n    }\n  };\n\n  PreservedAnalyses PA = PreservedAnalyses::all();\n\n  // Request PassInstrumentation from analysis manager, will use it to run\n  // instrumenting callbacks for the passes later.\n  // Here we use std::tuple wrapper over getResult which helps to extract\n  // AnalysisManager's arguments out of the whole ExtraArgs set.\n  PassInstrumentation PI =\n      detail::getAnalysisResult<PassInstrumentationAnalysis>(\n          AM, IR, std::tuple<ExtraArgTs...>(ExtraArgs...));\n\n  StackTraceEntry Entry(PI, IR);\n  for (auto &Pass : Passes) {\n    Entry.setPass(&*Pass);\n\n    // Check the PassInstrumentation's BeforePass callbacks before running the\n    // pass, skip its execution completely if asked to (callback returns\n    // false).\n    if (!PI.runBeforePass<IRUnitT>(*Pass, IR))\n      continue;\n\n    PreservedAnalyses PassPA = Pass->run(IR, AM, ExtraArgs...);\n\n    // Update the analysis manager as each pass runs and potentially\n    // invalidates analyses.\n    AM.invalidate(IR, PassPA);\n\n    // Call onto PassInstrumentation's AfterPass callbacks immediately after\n    // running the pass.\n    PI.runAfterPass<IRUnitT>(*Pass, IR, PassPA);\n\n    // Finally, intersect the preserved analyses to compute the aggregate\n    // preserved set for this pass manager.\n    PA.intersect(std::move(PassPA));\n  }\n\n  // Invalidation was handled after each pass in the above loop for the\n  // current unit of IR. Therefore, the remaining analysis results in the\n  // AnalysisManager are preserved. We mark this with a set so that we don't\n  // need to inspect each one individually.\n  PA.preserveSet<AllAnalysesOn<IRUnitT>>();\n\n  return PA;\n}\n\ntemplate <typename IRUnitT, typename... ExtraArgTs>\ninline AnalysisManager<IRUnitT, ExtraArgTs...>::AnalysisManager() = default;\n\ntemplate <typename IRUnitT, typename... ExtraArgTs>\ninline AnalysisManager<IRUnitT, ExtraArgTs...>::AnalysisManager(\n    AnalysisManager &&) = default;\n\ntemplate <typename IRUnitT, typename... ExtraArgTs>\ninline AnalysisManager<IRUnitT, ExtraArgTs...> &\nAnalysisManager<IRUnitT, ExtraArgTs...>::operator=(AnalysisManager &&) =\n    default;\n\ntemplate <typename IRUnitT, typename... ExtraArgTs>\ninline void\nAnalysisManager<IRUnitT, ExtraArgTs...>::clear(IRUnitT &IR,\n                                               llvm::StringRef Name) {\n  if (auto *PI = getCachedResult<PassInstrumentationAnalysis>(IR))\n    PI->runAnalysesCleared(Name);\n\n  auto ResultsListI = AnalysisResultLists.find(&IR);\n  if (ResultsListI == AnalysisResultLists.end())\n    return;\n  // Delete the map entries that point into the results list.\n  for (auto &IDAndResult : ResultsListI->second)\n    AnalysisResults.erase({IDAndResult.first, &IR});\n\n  // And actually destroy and erase the results associated with this IR.\n  AnalysisResultLists.erase(ResultsListI);\n}\n\ntemplate <typename IRUnitT, typename... ExtraArgTs>\ninline typename AnalysisManager<IRUnitT, ExtraArgTs...>::ResultConceptT &\nAnalysisManager<IRUnitT, ExtraArgTs...>::getResultImpl(\n    AnalysisKey *ID, IRUnitT &IR, ExtraArgTs... ExtraArgs) {\n  auto [RI, Inserted] = AnalysisResults.try_emplace(std::make_pair(ID, &IR));\n\n  // If we don't have a cached result for this function, look up the pass and\n  // run it to produce a result, which we then add to the cache.\n  if (Inserted) {\n    auto &P = this->lookUpPass(ID);\n\n    PassInstrumentation PI;\n    if (ID != PassInstrumentationAnalysis::ID()) {\n      PI = getResult<PassInstrumentationAnalysis>(IR, ExtraArgs...);\n      PI.runBeforeAnalysis(P, IR);\n    }\n\n    AnalysisResultListT &ResultList = AnalysisResultLists[&IR];\n    ResultList.emplace_back(ID, P.run(IR, *this, ExtraArgs...));\n\n    PI.runAfterAnalysis(P, IR);\n\n    // P.run may have inserted elements into AnalysisResults and invalidated\n    // RI.\n    RI = AnalysisResults.find({ID, &IR});\n    assert(RI != AnalysisResults.end() && \"we just inserted it!\");\n\n    RI->second = std::prev(ResultList.end());\n  }\n\n  return *RI->second->second;\n}\n\ntemplate <typename IRUnitT, typename... ExtraArgTs>\ninline void AnalysisManager<IRUnitT, ExtraArgTs...>::invalidate(\n    IRUnitT &IR, const PreservedAnalyses &PA) {\n  // We're done if all analyses on this IR unit are preserved.\n  if (PA.allAnalysesInSetPreserved<AllAnalysesOn<IRUnitT>>())\n    return;\n\n  // Track whether each analysis's result is invalidated in\n  // IsResultInvalidated.\n  SmallDenseMap<AnalysisKey *, bool, 8> IsResultInvalidated;\n  Invalidator Inv(IsResultInvalidated, AnalysisResults);\n  AnalysisResultListT &ResultsList = AnalysisResultLists[&IR];\n  for (auto &AnalysisResultPair : ResultsList) {\n    // This is basically the same thing as Invalidator::invalidate, but we\n    // can't call it here because we're operating on the type-erased result.\n    // Moreover if we instead called invalidate() directly, it would do an\n    // unnecessary look up in ResultsList.\n    AnalysisKey *ID = AnalysisResultPair.first;\n    auto &Result = *AnalysisResultPair.second;\n\n    auto IMapI = IsResultInvalidated.find(ID);\n    if (IMapI != IsResultInvalidated.end())\n      // This result was already handled via the Invalidator.\n      continue;\n\n    // Try to invalidate the result, giving it the Invalidator so it can\n    // recursively query for any dependencies it has and record the result.\n    // Note that we cannot reuse 'IMapI' here or pre-insert the ID, as\n    // Result.invalidate may insert things into the map, invalidating our\n    // iterator.\n    bool Inserted =\n        IsResultInvalidated.insert({ID, Result.invalidate(IR, PA, Inv)}).second;\n    (void)Inserted;\n    assert(Inserted && \"Should never have already inserted this ID, likely \"\n                       \"indicates a cycle!\");\n  }\n\n  // Now erase the results that were marked above as invalidated.\n  if (!IsResultInvalidated.empty()) {\n    for (auto I = ResultsList.begin(), E = ResultsList.end(); I != E;) {\n      AnalysisKey *ID = I->first;\n      if (!IsResultInvalidated.lookup(ID)) {\n        ++I;\n        continue;\n      }\n\n      if (auto *PI = getCachedResult<PassInstrumentationAnalysis>(IR))\n        PI->runAnalysisInvalidated(this->lookUpPass(ID), IR);\n\n      I = ResultsList.erase(I);\n      AnalysisResults.erase({ID, &IR});\n    }\n  }\n\n  if (ResultsList.empty())\n    AnalysisResultLists.erase(&IR);\n}\n} // end namespace llvm\n\n#endif // LLVM_IR_PASSMANAGERIMPL_H\n","numLines":223,"startLine":1,"totalLines":223}}}

The PassManager class ensures\n// that analysis results are available before a pass runs, and that Pass's are\n// destroyed when the PassManager is destroyed.\n//\n//===----------------------------------------------------------------------===//\n\n#ifndef LLVM_IR_LEGACYPASSMANAGER_H\n#define LLVM_IR_LEGACYPASSMANAGER_H\n\n#include \"llvm/Support/CBindingWrapping.h\"\n#include \"llvm/Support/Compiler.h\"\n\nnamespace llvm {\n\nclass Function;\nclass Pass;\nclass Module;\n\nnamespace legacy {\n\n// Whether or not -debug-pass has been specified. Key methods:\\n- `registerModuleAnalyses(ModuleAnalysisManager &MAM)` (PassBuilder.cpp:649): Registers all module-level analyses by expanding `PassRegistry.def`.\\n- `registerFunctionAnalyses()`, `registerCGSCCAnalyses()`, `registerLoopAnalyses()`: Similarly register analyses at each IR level.\\n- `crossRegisterProxies()`: Wires analysis managers together via proxy analyses.\\n- Extension point callbacks (e.g., `registerPeepholeEPCallback`, `registerVectorizerStartEPCallback`, etc.) allow plugins/targets to inject passes at specific pipeline positions.\\n\\n#### 6. Standard O2/O3 Optimization Pipeline (`llvm/lib/Passes/PassBuilderPipelines.cpp`)\\n\\nThe entry point for a standard compilation at O2/O3 is `PassBuilder::buildPerModuleDefaultPipeline(OptimizationLevel, ThinOrFullLTOPhase)` (line 1716). The execution order is:\\n\\n1. `Annotation2MetadataPass` — convert annotations to metadata.\\n2. `ForceFunctionAttrsPass` — apply forced function attributes.\\n3. `buildModuleSimplificationPipeline()` (line 1091) — inlining and canonicalization:\\n   - `InferFunctionAttrsPass`, `CoroEarlyPass`\\n   - Early FPM: `LowerExpectIntrinsicPass`, `SimplifyCFGPass`, `SROAPass`, `EarlyCSEPass`\\n   - `buildInlinerPipeline()` (line 942) — `ModuleInlinerWrapperPass` with CGSCC inliner\\n   - Post-inline function simplification\\n4. `buildModuleOptimizationPipeline()` (line 1478) — optimizations:\\n   - `EliminateAvailableExternallyPass`, `ReversePostOrderFunctionAttrsPass`\\n   - `RecomputeGlobalsAAPass`\\n   - Per-function: `Float2IntPass`, `LowerConstantIntrinsicsPass`, loop optimizations (LICM, vectorization via `LoopVectorizePass`, `SLPVectorizerPass`), `InstCombinePass`, `ADCEPass`, `SimplifyCFGPass`\\n   - O3-only: `ControlHeightReductionPass`, `ArgumentPromotionPass`\\n   - `GlobalDCEPass`, `ConstantMergePass`\\n\\nEach pipeline stage calls `MPM.addPass(...)` or `FPM.addPass(...)` to register passes into the pass manager, which are then all run in sequence when `PassManager::run()` is invoked on the module.\\n\\n---\\n\\n### Legacy Pass Manager (LPM)\\n\\n#### PassRegistry (`llvm/include/llvm/PassRegistry.h`, `llvm/lib/IR/PassRegistry.cpp`)\\n\\n`PassRegistry` is a global singleton (`PassRegistry::getPassRegistry()`) holding a map from type IDs and string names to `PassInfo` objects. It is populated at program startup via:\\n- `INITIALIZE_PASS(passName, arg, name, cfg, analysis)` macro (`llvm/include/llvm/PassSupport.h`, line 56): Expands to a static initializer function that calls `PassRegistry::registerPass(*PI, true)` (line 48).\\n- `RegisterPass<T>` template (`llvm/include/llvm/PassSupport.h`, line 89): A statically-allocated object whose constructor calls `PassRegistry::getPassRegistry()->registerPass(*this)`.\\n\\n#### PassInfo (`llvm/include/llvm/PassInfo.h`)\\n\\nStores the pass's string name, command-line arg, type ID, and a factory function (`NormalCtor_t`) for creating pass instances.\\n\\n#### Legacy PassManager (`llvm/include/llvm/IR/LegacyPassManager.h`, `llvm/lib/IR/LegacyPassManager.cpp`)\\n\\n- `legacy::PassManagerBase::add(Pass *P)` (line 49): Virtual method that enqueues a pass.\\n- `legacy::PassManager::add(Pass *P)` (line 59): Delegates to `PassManagerImpl`, which schedules passes respecting analysis dependencies from `PassRegistry`.\\n- `legacy::PassManager::run(Module &M)` (line 63): Runs all scheduled passes in order.\\n\\nThe legacy `add()` is the direct counterpart of the new PM's `addPass()`.\\n\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
